SELECT t."Id", t."Name", t."Stock", t."Price", t."CreatedDate", t."UpdatedDate", t0."Id", t0."CreatedDate", t0."Discriminator", t0."FileName", t0."FilePath", t0."Storage", t0."ProductImageFilesId", t0."ProductsId"

    ORDER BY p."CreatedDate" DESC
    LIMIT @__p_1 OFFSET @__p_0
) AS t
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT t1."Id", t1."CreatedDate", t1."Discriminator", t1."FileName", t1."FilePath", t1."Storage", p0."ProductImageFilesId", p0."ProductsId"

2023-11-12 20:13:14.037 +03:00 [INF] Executed DbCommand (20ms) [Parameters=[@__p_1='?' (DbType = Int32), @__p_0='?' (DbType = Int32)], CommandType='"Text"', CommandTimeout='30']
SELECT t."Id", t."Name", t."Stock", t."Price", t."CreatedDate", t."UpdatedDate", t1."Id", t1."CreatedDate", t1."Discriminator", t1."FileName", t1."FilePath", t1."Storage"
FROM (
    SELECT p."Id", p."Name", p."Stock", p."Price", p."CreatedDate", p."UpdatedDate"
    FROM "Products" AS p
    ORDER BY p."CreatedDate" DESC
    LIMIT @__p_1 OFFSET @__p_0
) AS t
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT t0."Id", t0."CreatedDate", t0."Discriminator", t0."FileName", t0."FilePath", t0."Storage", t0."ProductsId"
    FROM (
        SELECT t2."Id", t2."CreatedDate", t2."Discriminator", t2."FileName", t2."FilePath", t2."Storage", p0."ProductsId", ROW_NUMBER() OVER(PARTITION BY p0."ProductsId" ORDER BY p0."ProductImageFilesId", p0."ProductsId", t2."Id") AS row
        FROM "ProductProductImageFile" AS p0
        INNER JOIN (
            SELECT f."Id", f."CreatedDate", f."Discriminator", f."FileName", f."FilePath", f."Storage"
            FROM "Files" AS f
            WHERE f."Discriminator" = 'ProductImageFile'
        ) AS t2 ON p0."ProductImageFilesId" = t2."Id"
    ) AS t0
    WHERE t0.row <= 1
) AS t1 ON t."Id" = t1."ProductsId"
ORDER BY t."CreatedDate" DESC

SELECT t."Id", t."Name", t."Stock", t."Price", t."CreatedDate", t."UpdatedDate", t1."Id", t1."CreatedDate", t1."Discriminator", t1."FileName", t1."FilePath", t1."Storage"
FROM (
    SELECT p."Id", p."Name", p."Stock", p."Price", p."CreatedDate", p."UpdatedDate"
    FROM "Products" AS p
    ORDER BY p."CreatedDate" DESC
    LIMIT @__p_1 OFFSET @__p_0
) AS t
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT t0."Id", t0."CreatedDate", t0."Discriminator", t0."FileName", t0."FilePath", t0."Storage", t0."ProductsId"
    FROM (
        SELECT t2."Id", t2."CreatedDate", t2."Discriminator", t2."FileName", t2."FilePath", t2."Storage", p0."ProductsId", ROW_NUMBER() OVER(PARTITION BY p0."ProductsId" ORDER BY p0."ProductImageFilesId", p0."ProductsId", t2."Id") AS row
        FROM "ProductProductImageFile" AS p0
        INNER JOIN (
            SELECT f."Id", f."CreatedDate", f."Discriminator", f."FileName", f."FilePath", f."Storage"
            FROM "Files" AS f
            WHERE f."Discriminator" = 'ProductImageFile'
        ) AS t2 ON p0."ProductImageFilesId" = t2."Id"
    ) AS t0
    WHERE t0.row <= 1
) AS t1 ON t."Id" = t1."ProductsId"
ORDER BY t."CreatedDate" DESC

2023-11-12 20:18:43.062 +03:00 [INF] Executed DbCommand (2ms) [Parameters=[@__p_1='?' (DbType = Int32), @__p_0='?' (DbType = Int32)], CommandType='"Text"', CommandTimeout='30']
SELECT t."Id", t."Name", t."Stock", t."Price", t."CreatedDate", t."UpdatedDate", t1."Id", t1."CreatedDate", t1."Discriminator", t1."FileName", t1."FilePath", t1."Storage"
FROM (
    SELECT p."Id", p."Name", p."Stock", p."Price", p."CreatedDate", p."UpdatedDate"
    FROM "Products" AS p
    ORDER BY p."CreatedDate" DESC
    LIMIT @__p_1 OFFSET @__p_0
) AS t
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT t0."Id", t0."CreatedDate", t0."Discriminator", t0."FileName", t0."FilePath", t0."Storage", t0."ProductsId"
    FROM (
        SELECT t2."Id", t2."CreatedDate", t2."Discriminator", t2."FileName", t2."FilePath", t2."Storage", p0."ProductsId", ROW_NUMBER() OVER(PARTITION BY p0."ProductsId" ORDER BY p0."ProductImageFilesId", p0."ProductsId", t2."Id") AS row
        FROM "ProductProductImageFile" AS p0
        INNER JOIN (
            SELECT f."Id", f."CreatedDate", f."Discriminator", f."FileName", f."FilePath", f."Storage"
            FROM "Files" AS f
            WHERE f."Discriminator" = 'ProductImageFile'
        ) AS t2 ON p0."ProductImageFilesId" = t2."Id"
    ) AS t0
    WHERE t0.row <= 1
) AS t1 ON t."Id" = t1."ProductsId"
ORDER BY t."CreatedDate" DESC

2023-12-01 23:25:03.841 +03:00 [INF] Executed DbCommand (14ms) [Parameters=[@__p_1='?' (DbType = Int32), @__p_0='?' (DbType = Int32)], CommandType='"Text"', CommandTimeout='30']
SELECT t."Id", t."Name", t."Stock", t."Price", t."CreatedDate", t."UpdatedDate", t1."Id", t1."CreatedDate", t1."Discriminator", t1."FileName", t1."FilePath", t1."Storage"
FROM (
    SELECT p."Id", p."Name", p."Stock", p."Price", p."CreatedDate", p."UpdatedDate"
    FROM "Products" AS p
    ORDER BY p."CreatedDate" DESC
    LIMIT @__p_1 OFFSET @__p_0
) AS t
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT t0."Id", t0."CreatedDate", t0."Discriminator", t0."FileName", t0."FilePath", t0."Storage", t0."ProductsId"
    FROM (
        SELECT t2."Id", t2."CreatedDate", t2."Discriminator", t2."FileName", t2."FilePath", t2."Storage", p0."ProductsId", ROW_NUMBER() OVER(PARTITION BY p0."ProductsId" ORDER BY p0."ProductImageFilesId", p0."ProductsId", t2."Id") AS row
        FROM "ProductProductImageFile" AS p0
        INNER JOIN (
            SELECT f."Id", f."CreatedDate", f."Discriminator", f."FileName", f."FilePath", f."Storage"
            FROM "Files" AS f
            WHERE f."Discriminator" = 'ProductImageFile'
        ) AS t2 ON p0."ProductImageFilesId" = t2."Id"
    ) AS t0
    WHERE t0.row <= 1
) AS t1 ON t."Id" = t1."ProductsId"
ORDER BY t."CreatedDate" DESC

SELECT t."Id", t."Name", t."Stock", t."Price", t."CreatedDate", t."UpdatedDate", t1."Id", t1."CreatedDate", t1."Discriminator", t1."FileName", t1."FilePath", t1."Storage"
FROM (
    SELECT p."Id", p."Name", p."Stock", p."Price", p."CreatedDate", p."UpdatedDate"
    FROM "Products" AS p
    ORDER BY p."CreatedDate" DESC
    LIMIT @__p_1 OFFSET @__p_0
) AS t
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT t0."Id", t0."CreatedDate", t0."Discriminator", t0."FileName", t0."FilePath", t0."Storage", t0."ProductsId"
    FROM (
        SELECT t2."Id", t2."CreatedDate", t2."Discriminator", t2."FileName", t2."FilePath", t2."Storage", p0."ProductsId", ROW_NUMBER() OVER(PARTITION BY p0."ProductsId" ORDER BY p0."ProductImageFilesId", p0."ProductsId", t2."Id") AS row
        FROM "ProductProductImageFile" AS p0
        INNER JOIN (
            SELECT f."Id", f."CreatedDate", f."Discriminator", f."FileName", f."FilePath", f."Storage"
            FROM "Files" AS f
            WHERE f."Discriminator" = 'ProductImageFile'
        ) AS t2 ON p0."ProductImageFilesId" = t2."Id"
    ) AS t0
    WHERE t0.row <= 1
) AS t1 ON t."Id" = t1."ProductsId"
ORDER BY t."CreatedDate" DESC

2023-12-01 23:30:54.230 +03:00 [INF] Executed DbCommand (5ms) [Parameters=[@__p_1='?' (DbType = Int32), @__p_0='?' (DbType = Int32)], CommandType='"Text"', CommandTimeout='30']
SELECT t."Id", t."Name", t."Stock", t."Price", t."CreatedDate", t."UpdatedDate", t1."Id", t1."CreatedDate", t1."Discriminator", t1."FileName", t1."FilePath", t1."Storage"
FROM (
    SELECT p."Id", p."Name", p."Stock", p."Price", p."CreatedDate", p."UpdatedDate"
    FROM "Products" AS p
    ORDER BY p."CreatedDate" DESC
    LIMIT @__p_1 OFFSET @__p_0
) AS t
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT t0."Id", t0."CreatedDate", t0."Discriminator", t0."FileName", t0."FilePath", t0."Storage", t0."ProductsId"
    FROM (
        SELECT t2."Id", t2."CreatedDate", t2."Discriminator", t2."FileName", t2."FilePath", t2."Storage", p0."ProductsId", ROW_NUMBER() OVER(PARTITION BY p0."ProductsId" ORDER BY p0."ProductImageFilesId", p0."ProductsId", t2."Id") AS row
        FROM "ProductProductImageFile" AS p0
        INNER JOIN (
            SELECT f."Id", f."CreatedDate", f."Discriminator", f."FileName", f."FilePath", f."Storage"
            FROM "Files" AS f
            WHERE f."Discriminator" = 'ProductImageFile'
        ) AS t2 ON p0."ProductImageFilesId" = t2."Id"
    ) AS t0
    WHERE t0.row <= 1
) AS t1 ON t."Id" = t1."ProductsId"
ORDER BY t."CreatedDate" DESC
